## <a name="windows-server-2008"></a><span data-ttu-id="2dafd-1054">Windows Server 2008</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2dafd-1054">Windows Server 2008</span></span>

-   [<span data-ttu-id="2dafd-1055">Atributos</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2dafd-1055">Attributes</span></span>](#windows-server-2008-attributes)
